<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

That transcription was recorded by Jean Guillou on his cd "Organ Encores" on the Alpes d'Huez organ.

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Wir danken dir, Gott, wir danken dir
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">We thank thee, God, we thank thee
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca, es">Wir danken dir</span>

<tr>
<th>Authorities

<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 29
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 714
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 sections
<ol><li> Sinfonia (D major)
<dl><dd>after the "Preludio" (No.1) from <a href="/wiki/Violin_Partita_No.3_in_E_major,_BWV_1006_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Violin Partita No.3 in E major, BWV 1006 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)"><i>Violin Partita in E major, BWV 1006</i></a>
</dd></dl>
</li><li> [Coro]: Wir danken dir, Gott, wir danken dir (D major)
</li><li> Aria: Halleluja, Stärk und Macht (A major)
</li><li> Recitativo: Gottlob! es geht uns wohl! (F<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span> minor-B minor)
</li><li> Aria: Gedenk an uns mit deiner Liebe (B minor)
</li><li> Recitativo: Vergiß es ferner nicht, mit deiner Hand (D major)
</li><li> Arioso: Halleluja, Stärk und Macht (D major)
</li><li> Choral: Sei Lob und Preis mit Ehren (D major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
